FACILITY   (VDGT,2GERLMU) The experiments have been performed     D031000100011 
           with polarized deuterium beams delivered by the        D031000100012 
           Tandem accelerator of the University and               D031000100013 
           (VDGT,2GERMUN) Technical University in Munich. The     D031000100014 
           vector polarization P3 of the beam, obtained with an   D031000100015 
           atomic beam source was around 60%.                     D031000100016 
METHOD     (EDE)                                                  D031000100017 
DETECTOR   (COIN,MWPC,SWPC,SCIN) The reaction products were       D031000100018 
           analyzed at eleven angles between 6. and 35. degr.with D031000100019 
           the Munich Q3D spectrograph, and then detected in a    D031000100020 
           1.8 m long focal plane detector consisted of a         D031000100021 
           multiwire detector, two single wire detectors and      D031000100022 
           plastic scintillator in coincidence.                   D031000100023 
ANALYSIS   For each angle two runs were measured, with spin 'up'  D031000100024 
           and 'down', respectively. For each peak in the         D031000100025 
           spectrum, and at each angle, both the differential     D031000100026 
           cross section and the analyzing power were determined. D031000100027 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-S) Statistical error                              D031000100028
